Domestic Important Telegrams

Two Armies Face Off Across the Railway in Yuguan 13

Japanese troops dig trenches and advance towards Yuguan in large numbers. Unreasonable demands raised by the Japanese side were sternly rejected by He Zhuguo. The Central Government orders Zhang Xueliang to deal with the incident with force. (Peiping) Japanese troops south of the Yuguan railway, our troops north of it, both sides in confrontation (12th Special Dispatch) (Nanjing) According to today's Tianjin telegram, the Japanese vanguard is only eight miles from Shanhaiguan and continues to advance towards the Chinese defense line. Japanese troops are also digging trenches in the Hongqiangzi area, five miles from Yuguan. Furthermore, Japanese troops have dismantled railway tracks in the Changli area south of Yuguan. Armored trains from the south have reached Suizhong, only one station away from Yuguan (12th Reuters Telegram).

He Zhuguo Meets with Japanese Military Officers 14

(Peiping) Due to repeated provocations by Japanese troops, He Zhuguo arranged to meet with Japanese military officers to discuss solutions. The meeting took place at the Fuxingju Restaurant at 5:00 PM on the 10th. Three representatives from our side, including He Zhuguo, attended, as well as three representatives from the Japanese garrison, including the head of the military police. The Japanese side insisted on the right to freely suppress bandits within eighty miles of Yuguan and demanded to borrow important passes such as Jioumenkou and Shimenzhai. He Zhuguo sternly rejected these demands, and the meeting ended without result (12th Special Dispatch).

Japanese Troops Open Fire Late at Night in Yuguan 15

(Peiping) A person from Yuguan reported that at 11:00 PM on the 9th, over 300 Japanese soldiers in the Japanese barracks fired rifles, machine guns, and mortars until 1:30 AM. He Zhuguo sent a staff officer to question them, and the commander of the Japanese garrison claimed that there were bandits 15 miles west of Yuguan that they intended to suppress, but in reality, there were no bandits (12th Special Dispatch). (Peiping) On the afternoon of the 10th, a puppet flag was suddenly discovered outside the east wall of Yuguan Station. Over 100 Japanese soldiers, led by the commander of the garrison, and over 100 puppet police, led by the Chinese Guan Shanxian, conducted drills and fired guns near the station, causing great fear among the residents. He Zhuguo has moved into the old site of the Yudu Tong Yamen (12th Special Dispatch).

Central Government Sends Reply Telegram to Zhang Xueliang 16

(Nanjing) Zhang Xueliang telegraphed the Central Government about the situation of Japanese troops attempting to disturb Shanhaiguan and requested instructions on strategy. The Central Government replied, ordering him to respond with force according to the planned strategy (12th Special Dispatch).

He Zhuguo Discusses the Situation in Yuguan 17

(Peiping) Yuguan telegram: He Zhuguo told reporters that Yuguan has become increasingly important since the September 18th Incident. The commander of the Japanese garrison, Matsushita, recently used the excuse of preventing insurgents to demand the freedom to suppress them in writing, forcing him to sign and making threatening remarks. He has a responsibility to defend the territory, stopping unauthorized actions and protecting overseas Chinese. The troops defending Yuguan are all well-trained. Recently, over 80 puppet police arrived in the pass, claiming to maintain the puppet Fengshan Road, without prior notification, which is a transgression. He only knows of the nation. He is negotiating about the Japanese troops opening fire, which affects security, and hopes to resolve it (12th Special Dispatch).

Rumor That Wang Shuchang Commands the Front Lines 18

(Tianjin) Zhang Xueliang appointed Wang Shuchang, commander of the Second Army, as the commander-in-chief of the Northeastern anti-rebellion and punitive expedition yesterday. All the troops stationed in the Shanhaiguan-Tianjin area, approximately six armies, are under his command (12th Dentsu Telegram).

Japanese Troops Reconnoiter Along the Beining Line 19

(Peiping) Japanese troops, in groups of thirty or twenty, frequently board the 101st and 102nd trains on the Beining Railway to reconnoiter at various stations along the line. Rumors in Yuguan are rife, and the situation is becoming increasingly tense (12th Special Dispatch).

Most of the Japanese Troops are Concentrated in Suizhong 20

(Peiping) Japanese troops have been busy moving troops and weapons towards the Zhongqian Suo area in recent days and building defensive works in Wanjatun and other places. The outposts have reached Hongqiangzi, and most of the troops are concentrated in Suizhong. The Japanese garrison stationed in Yuguan has been adding sandbags and electric fences near the barracks (12th Special Dispatch).

Several Japanese Warships Anchored Between Qinhuangdao and Yuguan 21

(Peiping) Several Japanese warships are anchored between Qinhuangdao and Yuguan, constantly patrolling back and forth. Japanese troops in Yuguan are frequently provoking our side (12th Special Dispatch).

Japanese Embassy Denies Troop Increase in Yuguan 22

(Peiping) The spokesperson of the Japanese Embassy told a Reuters reporter today that the rumor that there would be an incident in Yuguan is unfounded. The report in the Chinese newspaper that Japan has dispatched a division of troops to Yuguan is completely baseless. Japan has not increased the number of troops stationed there, which is currently less than two hundred, and has no intention of increasing them. As for the rumor that a Japanese fleet was discovered outside Qinhuangdao, this is because the Japanese fleet in Lushunkou conducts large-scale exercises every spring, which often take place along the coast from Yantai to Qingdao, before returning to Lushunkou. The fleet is currently conducting its annual exercises (12th Reuters Telegram). Ma Zhanshan's Army

Advancing Towards Heihe 23

Defeated Japanese troops at Taha Station Sent planes to bomb Heihe. (Peiping) Harbin, November 11th Telegram: Ma Zhanshan recently deployed a force of 25,000 men along the Qiqihar-Krestovozdvizhenka railroad line, gradually advancing toward the capital of Longjiang Province. On the 10th, they encountered a Japanese unit near Taha Station, a branch line of the railroad, and engaged in battle. As a result, the Japanese army was defeated, suffering heavy casualties, with the remainder in full retreat. Furthermore, Ma has scheduled a general offensive on Heihe before the 15th. The airfield has been completed, and on the morning of the 10th, three aircraft were dispatched to bomb Heihe, causing panic among puppet government officials and residents. The commander of the Japanese military division, Domon, has reinforced the area by dispatching an entire brigade to assist in the defense (12th Central News Agency Telegram).

Fighting on the Eastern Chinese and Hailun Railroads 24

(Harbin) Fresh Japanese troops continue to arrive daily from various locations in the south. Fighting is ongoing northeast of Harbin. The transportation between Hailin and Mudanjiang, in the eastern section of the Eastern Chinese Railroad,

Page 6

has now been cut off. The tracks have been dismantled. Chinese and Japanese troops are currently engaged in fierce fighting, with reports of numerous deaths and injuries. Two Russian engineers and drivers of a Japanese armored train have also been injured. Fighting is also taking place near the Hailun railroad north of Harbin. The atmosphere of chaos is intensifying. Four villages along the Songhua River, less than nine miles from Harbin, have all been burned. Reports suggest they were looted (12th Reuters Telegram).

Japanese 14th Division Arrives in Harbin 25

(Harbin) The majority of the Japanese 14th Division, which was transferred from Shanghai, has arrived. Division commander Matsumoto arrived in Harbin yesterday. The 14th Division is relieving the 10th Division of Hirose. The 1st Division of Hirose has been deployed along the Songhua River, but the destination is unknown. Last night, a unit of the 14th Division engaged in battle with Chinese troops at Wujimi River on the Eastern Chinese Railroad, driving back approximately 600 Chinese soldiers. Li Haiqing's unit, approximately 6,000 men, retreated north after withdrawing from Nongan. It is expected that this unit will reach the western section of the Eastern Chinese Railroad when the League of Nations investigation team leaves Harbin for Qiqihar, which is causing some anxiety (12th Reuters Telegram). (Peiping) The entire Japanese 14th Division, which withdrew from Shanghai, landed in Yingkou yesterday and will proceed to Suizhong (12th Special Dispatch).

Three Provinces National Highway Plan 45

Foreign Important Telegrams 85

Funeral of the Deceased French President Held 86

Representatives from over forty countries participated in the funeral procession. The procession was two miles long, solemn and respectful. ▲Guomin News Agency, Paris, 12th: Today, the funeral of the deceased French President Doumer was held. The whole country suspended work to mourn. The hearse left the Presidential Palace at 8:07 in the morning. The procession was about two miles long. Representatives from over forty countries attended the funeral procession, including the King of Belgium, the Prince of Wales of the United Kingdom, the Duke of Aosta of Italy, and Prince Paul of Yugoslavia, all of whom were closely protected by guards. The coffin was placed on an open hearse, drawn by eight black horses, led by thousands of cavalry, and followed by lawyers in gowns, members of the French Academy, members of both houses of parliament, and representatives of the people. The new President Lebrun, accompanied by Doumer's family, closely followed the hearse. The Belgian King and the British Prince and other dignitaries and the diplomatic corps were behind the family. Troops stood guard along the road, and saluted with their guns when the hearse passed. Hundreds of thousands of people gathered behind the troops, all taking off their hats and sobbing. At 9:30, they arrived at Notre Dame Cathedral, where Cardinal Verdi conducted a Mass and prayed. After the prayer, they went to the Pantheon, where Prime Minister Tardieu delivered a eulogy. (The following is a Havas dispatch.) He highly praised the deceased president's personality and said that the murderer's actions aroused unanimous indignation. Afterwards, Doumer's life experience, from the beginning of his prominence to his appointment as head of state, was narrated one by one. Tardieu especially praised the deceased president's political achievements during his tenure as Governor-General of Vietnam. He said, (Although Mr. Doumer was old and had experienced grief, he still did not avoid difficulties and worked hard for the country, serving as Minister of Finance twice, then being appointed as Speaker of the Senate, and finally enjoying the glory of head of state.) In his conclusion, Mr. Tai also said, (The death of President Doumer is no less than the death of a warrior on the battlefield. There are still two responsibilities that he has left to us. Mr. Doumer was humble throughout his life, so we can only work hard to fulfill this mission in order to repay Mr. Doumer. The so-called two responsibilities are: one is to help his family with our sincere respect, and the other is to unite and work hard to enable France to fulfill its mission.) ▲Reuters, Paris, 12th: The road that the funeral procession of the deceased President Doumer will pass through was lined with people in the morning to express their grief and respect. His remains were first moved from the Presidential Palace to the Pantheon, where Tardieu delivered the funeral speech, and then stopped at Notre Dame Cathedral, where the Bishop of Paris performed the funeral rites. The procession was half a mile long, led by the Republican Guard cavalry and infantry and retired soldiers, followed by seven cars full of wreaths, one of which was red roses, which was a gift from the British Emperor, followed by a black silver hearse, drawn by six black horses, with four people on each side as escorts, followed by Doumer's family, all walking, followed by the new President Lebrun, the King of Belgium, the British Prince, other foreign representatives, members of the Tardieu Cabinet, members of the diplomatic corps, and members of both houses of parliament, all following the funeral procession. The whole team moved slowly and was unusually quiet. Only the sound of the army band playing mourning music and the sound of horses' hooves were heard along the way. After the ceremony at Notre Dame Cathedral, the team reassembled and slowly circled the Cluny Museum and reached the Pantheon, placing the coffin on the top of the wide steps. After a while, it will be moved to the Doumer family cemetery in Vaux-Villars. Two of Doumer's four sons who died in battle in the European War are also buried there. After arriving at the Pantheon, Tardieu, from the left of the burial niche, that is, the place where his cabinet colleagues stood, went to the right of the burial niche. The family members of the deceased president were all tearfully watching the coffin there. Mr. Tai then addressed Mrs. Doumer to comfort her. The scene at that time was very moving. Mr. Tai then ascended the platform and praised the deceased president's deeds during his lifetime for twenty minutes. At that time, the Paris garrison, led by General Chaulot, marched in a parade, and the military appearance was very impressive. It lasted for forty-five minutes. After the new president and the royal family members left the Pantheon, the coffin was placed on the hearse again and carried to the Vaux-Villars cemetery. The Doumer family and members of the cabinet were followed. The funeral was very simple. ▲Guomin News Agency, Paris, 11th: The British Prince of Wales, the King of Belgium, Prince Paul of Yugoslavia, Prince Xue Gewa of Sweden, and others arrived here tonight to attend the funeral of the deceased French President Doumer tomorrow. Many famous politicians and nobles from European countries also came here to attend the funeral. Germany sent the Dutch Ambassador to France, Cardinal Chu, as the representative of the country and the president personally. ▲Reuters, Nanjing, 12th: Dr. Yan Huiqing, the chief representative of China to the League of Nations, represented China in Paris today to participate in the funeral of the deceased President Doumer. ▲Reuters, London, 12th: A memorial service was held for the deceased French President Doumer at Westminster Abbey today. The palace and government offices were all flying flags at half-mast.

Foreign Important Telegrams Two

The Murderer of Doumer 87

Gogulov's Confession 88

▲Havas, Paris, 11th: Gogulov, the murderer of Doumer, was interrogated again yesterday in front of his lawyer. Gogulov slowly pleaded and recounted his life experience, which took a long time.

Head Injured During the European War 89

He is the son of a small wealthy villager. He was injured in the head during the European War and received the St. George Medal twice. During the Russian Revolution, he joined the anti-Soviet Cossack secret organization. His father was killed by the Bolsheviks during a riot. He escaped into the mountains and was spared.

Joined the Socialist Revolutionary Party 90

Later, he returned to Minsk and joined the anti-Bolshevik organization led by Savinkov (Savinkov was the former commander of the Socialist Revolutionary Party's combat brigade). Then, because the Cheka (political police bureau) was searching very urgently, he fled to Poland in 1921.

Accused of Abortion Case 91

He then went to Prague, the capital of Czechoslovakia, where he obtained a medical degree. Later, he was accused of performing an abortion and left Czechoslovakia. He claimed that the abortion case was a false accusation.

Kidnapping Lindbergh's Son is Fabricated 92

As for the notes found on him, the matters recorded on them, such as claiming that Lindbergh's son was kidnapped by him, Gogulov admitted that they were fabricated. The reason for writing this was to seek the death penalty.

Intended to Assassinate Political Leaders 93

He also said that in 1929 he intended to assassinate Hindenburg, but failed to obtain a passport to Germany. He also planned to assassinate the Czech President Masaryk, but when he met Masaryk, he found him to be exceptionally kind and could not bring himself to do it. Gogulov said that he intended to fight against everything. Lenin and the Soviet Russian Ambassador to France were all people he wanted to assassinate. Because he could not go to Moscow, and the Soviet Russian Ambassador to France refused to meet him, he could not realize his plans. The court will carefully verify Gogulov's new confession.

Leader of the Green Russians Implicated 94

▲Havas, Berlin, 11th: At the request of the Paris police, the Berlin police interrogated the Russian expatriate Yakovlev today. This person is the editor of the "Tuxang" newspaper published in Paris and Berlin, which is the organ of the "Green Russians." Yakovlev confessed that he did not communicate with Gogulov often, but admitted to being the leader of the anti-Soviet party. In this capacity, he tried to persuade Gogulov and Gogulov's friends to join his party. Yakovlev will continue to be interrogated.

Naval Maneuvers on the Pacific Ocean 97

Over a hundred warships participated. Large airship lands in San Diego. A sudden gust of wind killed two people. ▲Guomin News Agency, San Francisco, 11th: The US battleship fleet was delayed due to the large naval airship Akron encountering strong winds and rain along the way, and it was unable to arrive here on the originally scheduled date to meet the fleet. It has now been temporarily decided to cancel the joint maneuvers of the airship and the battleship fleet. The fleet is still scheduled to depart from here alone tomorrow. It is reported that 141 US ships have been concentrated in the Pacific since March 23 to practice a simulated naval battle to attack important ports in the Pacific. It will be completed on Thursday, followed by a large fleet gathering outside the port of Los Angeles. After this, the battleship fleet will return to various bases in Southern California, and the patrol fleet will still take the Panama route back to the Atlantic Ocean, and is scheduled to arrive in New York on June 10. ▲Japan United Press, San Francisco, 11th: The US Navy will hold its annual large-scale exercise in the Pacific Ocean starting on May 18. Over a hundred warships and 40,000 personnel will participate in the maneuvers. It encountered wind along the way. When it landed here, 200 sailors worked hard to climb the ropes released by the airship, intending to tie up the airship. Unexpectedly, a gust of wind suddenly rose, blowing the airship into the sky. As a result, except for three people, everyone who climbed the ropes let go, and three people who did not let go of the ropes swayed in the air at a height of 200 feet, and then fell to the ground and died due to exhaustion. Although firefighters ran under the airship, holding nets to try to save them, they were unable to save them in time. The third person desperately tried to hook the ropes with both feet, and was pulled into the ship by people in the airship, thus escaping the disaster.

Disarmament Conference 98

Discussing the Caliber of Cannons 99

Britain, the United States, France, and Japan all advocated. The largest caliber can reach 15 centimeters. Small countries, with Italy and Russia as their leaders. Strive to abolish large cannons of 10 centimeters.

Germany Demands Equality in Armaments 100

▲Guomin News Agency, Geneva, 11th: Today, the Land Armaments Committee of the Disarmament Conference discussed from 10:15 a.m. to 12:30 p.m. what caliber of cannons are defensive and which are used exclusively for aggression, but each still held its own opinion and it was difficult to reach a compromise. Small countries, with Italy and Russia as their leaders, strove to abolish cannons with a caliber of over 100 mm (i.e. 10 cm). China advocated that the cannons used for defense should be limited to 80 mm. Germany requested that they be limited to 77 mm. Britain, the United States, France, Japan, and others supported that the largest caliber could reach 155 mm. ▲Reuters, Berlin, 11th: Today, German Chancellor Brüning stated in the Reichstag that Germany is determined not to remain in its current unequal position on the issue of armaments. Brüning solemnly stated that although Germany does not want to increase armaments to the same extent as other countries, it wants to obtain an equal position. Germany disarmed after the European War, but the military equipment in Europe has increased compared to before the war. The German Chancellor stated that the three issues of disarmament, reparations, and economic crisis are closely related, and the fate of the world in the future depends on the direction of their resolution. ▲Guomin News Agency, Geneva, 11th: Today, a group of news media representatives visited Hansson, the chairman of the Disarmament Conference, and expressed their dissatisfaction with the secret meetings of the various committees of the Disarmament Conference, because if there is no real information available, they have to use hearsay as news material. Hansson has promised to find a way to improve.

The United States on Japan 106

Another Clear Statement 107

▲ Undersecretary of State's Speech at International Law Conference ▲ Non-recognition of new territories acquired in violation of the Pact of Paris ▲ Also said the government cannot stop citizens from rejecting foreign goods Osaka Asahi Shimbun, Washington Special Telegram: US Undersecretary of State Mr. Clark Yossel, on the 5th, at the International Law Conference, promoted the Hoover Doctrine and gave a speech on the new US foreign policy. His speech attracted much attention from various countries. The gist of it is translated as follows: Mr. Clark said that the US State Department's note to China and Japan on January 8 and the letter from Stimson to Senator Borah on February 13 were intended to materialize and promote their realization. In other words, the United States absolutely does not recognize new territories acquired in violation of the Kellogg-Briand Pact, and this is the fundamental concept of diplomacy. Originally, the method of preventing war was the use of force to prevent war, which was included in the Covenant of the League of Nations, but the Pact of Paris made no mention of it at all. However, recently, the method of coercion against countries that do not abide by the Kellogg Pact is to advocate economic sanctions. This concept is also implied in the Covenant of the League of Nations, so the US government is extremely opposed to it for fear of inciting war. However, the United States takes this as a prerequisite and wants to realize the effect of the Hoover Doctrine, that is, President Hoover is concerned about improving future international relations, and completely regards any result obtained through war as invalid. This is a strict policy of using force, but this doctrine does not seem to correct the current injustices in the world. However, according to the meaning of the Kellogg Pact to prevent war, and without the danger of war arising from economic sanctions, it is a peaceful and effective sanction. Therefore, I firmly believe that the Hoover Doctrine will be welcomed by our people and is a fair foundation in international law. Mr. Clark also said that there is no relationship between official boycotts and individual voluntary boycotts. Recalling when the United States was in World War I, the majority of the people rejected German goods, but the US government could not order individual citizens to suppress their non-boycott and force them to buy German goods, etc. Mr. Clark was an important figure in the United States. Since Stimson has not yet returned to the country, he has become the head of the foreign affairs authority. Now that he has published this policy at an authoritative international law conference, its relationship with our country is very significant and can be imagined. The League of Nations Investigation Team arrived in Shenyang and took a train to Changchun. The photo shows them disembarking at Gongzhuling to visit an agricultural experiment field. The standing person is Gu Weijun, and the person bowing is General Claut.

Detailed Account of the Red Bandits' Invasion of Longyan and Zhangzhou 112

▲ The number of bandits is actually only over 8,000. Special correspondence: The red bandits from western Fujian who invaded Longyan and Zhangzhou have been reported in previous newspapers. Here, we will further describe the actual situation obtained from the battlefield as follows: ▲ The Fall of Longyan The bandits who attacked Fujian this time were the pseudo-Fifth Army Corps, the Fourth Army, the Twelfth Army, the Thirteenth Army, the Fifteenth Army, and the pseudo-Independent Division, the pseudo-Thirty-seventh Division, and the pseudo-Thirty-eighth Division, totaling nine divisions. The pseudo-Fourth Army was led by Lin Biao, the pseudo-Twelfth Army was Luo Binghui's unit, the pseudo-Thirteenth Army was Zuo Quan's unit, and the pseudo-Fifteenth Army was Sun Bu's rebel army, with Li Zhentong as the army commander. These various forces claimed to have more than 10,000 people, but in reality, there were only over 8,000 people, with 6,000 to 7,000 guns. They all raised the flags of the Chinese Workers' and Peasants' Red Army of the 某軍 某師. Reuters reported that it was the black-bordered red-hearted National Salvation Party flag, which was a false rumor. On April 9, the bandit army arrived at Dachi (a district of Longyan). On the morning of the 10th, they captured Xiaochi and went straight to Kao Tang, contacting the 291st Regiment of Zhang Zhen's 49th Division at Shipaiqian Longmen (15 miles from the city of Yan). The fighting was fierce. Although the bandits suffered heavy casualties, the 291st Regiment was isolated and suffered almost half its losses. At that time, Battalion Commander Wang Siyuan was captured, and Deputy Regiment Commander Li was killed in battle. Because the bandits were fierce, they could not resist, and Longmen was occupied. At the same time, another part of the bandits went straight to the county seat by抄径道 from Tongbo. Because there were no soldiers guarding the area, the bandits were able to drive straight in and approach the city. The Independent Regiment stationed outside the West Gate counterattacked in a hurry, causing chaos in the city. As a result, the Independent Regiment also suffered losses. Regiment Commander Zhang Xingbai was injured, and many company and platoon leaders were also killed or wounded. That night, Yang Fengnian, commander of the 145th Brigade, led the entire force to retreat to the Lantian Shantou area of Shizhong and camped. The next day, they shortened the defense line again and retreated to the area between Longshan and Mashan to deploy defenses. Shizhong was only guarded by Xie Yangqi's unit of the First Security Brigade and the militia who retreated from Longyan. The bandits wanted to attack Zhangzhou, so Shizhong bore the brunt. ▲ The Long Battle of Shizhong At dawn on the 13th, the red bandits used all of their 8,000-plus troops to besiege Shizhong from the east, west, and north. The security team and the militia rose up to meet the enemy. Because all the defensive works had not yet been fully prepared, the fighting was quite difficult. The bandit army used artillery and machine guns to cover their reckless charge. Fortunately, the soldiers of the team responded calmly and fought fiercely from morning to night. The bandits did not succeed in the end, and they suffered heavy casualties. The government troops seized more than a dozen Type 65 rifles and many other military supplies, so they collapsed and retreated. The bandits, unable to capture Shizhong, went straight to Zhangzhou on the morning of the 14th by抄径道, and the entire pseudo-Thirty-eighth Division guarded Shanglai Niubi Kong (separated by a mountain from the boundary of Shizhong) to contain Shizhong and prevent it from copying their rear, and to intimidate it. They bombarded Shizhong with artillery and machine guns every day. To this day, for more than two weeks, there has not been a day without fierce fighting. On the 16th and 17th, the bandits used night battles to charge recklessly, also with machine guns and artillery cover. The gunfire was also very fierce, especially the battle on the 19th was the most intense. The bandits went straight from Xishan to the Zuokeng Yangliu Si Dazhong Bridge position. Both sides engaged in close combat. Xie Yangqiu, deputy captain of the security team, took the lead and charged in a melee, killing more than 30 bandits and wounding more than 100, and seizing more than 20 Type 65 and 79 rifles, more than 30 hand grenades, more than a dozen broadswords (used by the broadsword team), and countless other military supplies. Since that battle, there have only been artillery battles. The government soldiers are extremely calm. The previous rumors that Shizhong and Zhangping had fallen are all false. The bandits have suffered repeated heavy casualties, with more than half of their men killed or wounded, and their arrogance has been frustrated. However, in order to maintain their connection between Zhangzhou and Longyan, they have to desperately defend Shanglai and use attack as defense to try to contain Shizhong. ▲ The Fall of Zhangzhou The red bandits, unable to capture Shizhong, used most of their forces to attack Zhangzhou by 抄径道. Starting on the 15th, they contacted the 49th Division at Mashan. The bandits were unsuccessful and went out of Yongfeng to Danai and袭取 Nanjin County. The rear of the 49th Division was surrounded, so it retreated to Zhao'an Pinghe. In a hurry, the losses were quite large. Chen Qifang, commander of the 292nd Regiment, was killed in battle, and two battalion commanders were killed in battle. Many company and platoon leaders were injured. After this setback, Zhangzhou was finally undefended. The bandits looted very cruelly along the way. They demanded 1 million yuan in Zhangzhou and 400,000 yuan in Shima. Reuters reported that the bandits did not harass the people along the way, which is also a false rumor. ▲ Recent Situation The Zhang bandits are now dividing their forces to迫漳浦诏安, with one part disturbing Anxi and Tong'an, trying to窜泉永. The bandits in Yan number about 1,000 people. There are also about 1,000 people in Shanglai, attached with artillery teams and machine gun companies. There are about 200-plus in Hekei, and there are also 200-300 people in Shuichao Jinshan Longshan and other places. There are about 500-plus in Shancheng. A part has already disturbed the Chuanchang Shangxiafeng, and the bandits in Hekei also entered Yongxi Bingliao today. Currently, the militia in the Kuiyang Changjiao area have stepped up their guard. At the same time, the Longtan Fushi Dapengkang Mayor Liukongfu and the people's protection teams of the 18 townships of Jinfeng, as well as the people's protection teams of the three districts of Nanjin, Kuiyang Quanlongshan Hekei Zhangping Yongfu, and the Longyan Quan屬保衛團, the First Security Brigade of Shizhong, etc., are forming a large-scale alliance to jointly suppress the bandits, and they have sent representatives to be stationed in various townships for liaison. As for the Guangdong army's assistance to Fujian, in addition to Huang Renhuan's division already concentrating in Hangcheng and advancing towards Yan, Huang Yanzhen's division has also arrived in Yongding, and the vanguard has been stationed in Hulei. If they can lead the army to advance rapidly, it will not be difficult to recover Yan and Zhangzhou in a short period of time. (May 2) Local Correspondence

▲ Another Robbery Case at Maihua Bridge At Maihua Bridge, more than ten miles northeast of the city, on the evening of the 10th, more than ten people armed with bayonets and ropes broke open the door of farmer Lu Haijin's house, tied up all five members of the family, and searched the place thoroughly. Suzhou 114

▲ Difficulty in Collecting Rent The Wu County Government was ordered to collect two months' rent, and County Chief Zou hired Xu Yu'e and 43 others as rent solicitation committee members to form a rent solicitation committee. Later, the meeting decided to collect rents for May and July, half of which would be sent to the province and half of which would be retained in the county. However, the entire rent solicitation committee wrote to the county government yesterday, stating that the Suzhou area was indirectly affected by the Shanghai war, and the people suffered heavy losses. They really have no ability to bear the burden, and asked to be exempted from the collection in order to relieve the people's strength. The landlords are now coming forward through their real estate colleagues to notify the tenants to postpone the payment of rent. The county government will submit a report to the province for approval and implementation.

Wuxi 115

▲ Silk Factories Are on the Verge of Bankruptcy The silk factory industry in Wuxi has been failing for years, and most of them are on the verge of bankruptcy. Even a few that are struggling to support themselves have completely stopped production. Since the outbreak of the Shanghai war, financial transactions in various places have been suspended, and commercial accounts have been extended from the end of February to the end of May. Now, the deadline is approaching, and the amount of money owed by the silk factory industry to the silver and money industries is particularly large. In the current situation, it is really impossible to repay. Moreover, the new silkworms are about to be on the market, and each factory needs a large amount of cash if it needs to collect silkworms. The money used in this year's silkworm market has had a huge impact. Yesterday, silk factory colleagues held a special meeting to discuss the results of the rescue measures: (1) The Silk Factory Association will forward a letter to the Money Industry Association, requesting that it consider the fact that the silk factory industry is on the verge of bankruptcy and allow the debts owed to be reduced in interest and repaid slowly. (2) As the new silkworms are about to be on the market, please ask each bank to consider lending money according to the resolutions of the Shanghai Congress so that each factory can start collecting silkworms and maintain the rural economy, and the workers in each factory can also rely on it to maintain their livelihoods. (3) In terms of business, those factories that have signed leases with the industrial sector have a deposit of thousands of yuan as a rule. Now, because of the suspension of business in the middle, the rent cannot be paid as usual. They should immediately discuss with the industrial sector and completely exempt the rent from January to April of this year.

Xinghua 119

▲ The Miserable Situation of the Xinghua Disaster Victims Since the city was hit by a major flood, although general disaster victims have received emergency winter and spring relief three times, and soup kitchens have been established to distribute porridge for relief, due to the excessive severity of the disaster, it is a drop in the bucket. Most of the general disaster victims now use bamboo edges, grass sprouts, small garlic, and other grasses as food because they have no grain to eat. The miserable situation is unbearable to witness. In addition, there is no hope for the spring harvest, and there will be grain only in the autumn harvest. The days to come are long, how can we bear it? We hope that the relief authorities will quickly seek a solution for relief, which may save the disaster victims who are about to die.

Hangzhou 122

▲ The Tobacco Disaster in the Taizhou Area of Eastern Zhejiang The Taizhou area of eastern Zhejiang is located near the sea, and the customs are strong. Farmers privately plant tobacco seedlings in the countryside, which is everywhere. Although the counties of Linhai, Huangyan, Wenling, Tiantai, Xianju, Ninghai, etc. have repeatedly received provincial orders to ban them, farmers collude with bandits and continue to disobey in public and comply in private, which is really difficult to prevent. Now is the early summer season, which is the time for planting tobacco seedlings. The county heads of the counties in the area, in order to eliminate the scourge of drugs, have jointly telegraphed the provincial government, the Civil Affairs Department, and the Security Office yesterday, requesting that an artillery company be dispatched to Taizhou to assist in inspecting the villages in order to eliminate the tobacco atmosphere.

Education News

News

This Year's Summer Vacation Primary and Secondary Schools 123

Graduates Will Have a Joint Examination 124

▲ Ministry of Education Meeting Regulations ▲ Promulgated After Textual Amendments On the afternoon of the 11th, the Ministry of Education held a ministry affairs meeting. The Vice Ministers, various department heads, counselors, and section chiefs attended. Minister Zhu presided over the meeting and discussed (the draft regulations for the joint examination of primary and secondary school graduates). The clauses of the draft were revised and passed one by one. The general idea is that in order to standardize the graduation level of students in public and private primary, junior high, and senior high schools, and to improve teaching efficiency, after the current graduates of primary and secondary schools have passed the examination by the original school, the education administrative organs of each province, city, district, and county will organize a joint examination committee for primary and secondary school graduates to preside over all joint examination matters. The ministry will also stipulate the joint examination subjects. The method, location, and method of calculating scores of the joint examination will be stipulated in detail by the主管教育行政機關 and submitted to the ministry for record and implementation. The remaining clauses will be officially promulgated and ordered to all provinces and cities to hold them uniformly before the summer vacation of this year after the Ministry of Education adds detailed revisions. Preparations for the Takeover of School and Cultural Institutions 126

▲Today and tomorrow, responsible personnel must be sent to the Education Bureau to register for the takeover by the Municipal War Zone Consolidation and the soon-to-be troop-withdrawn zone takeover committees. Mr. and Mrs. Rogers Visit the Shanghai Art College 127

▲Discussing the Highest Principles of Chinese Painting with Liu Haisu. Dr. Rogers, an American educator, was specially dispatched to China by the US government to investigate education. He has stayed in Shanghai for a long time, making precise observations of our country's cultural undertakings. He also pays great attention to Oriental art. Yesterday afternoon at 2 p.m., accompanied by Director Xu of the Municipal Education Bureau, he visited the college to explore Chinese art. The college professors led them to visit the classrooms and observe Western and Chinese painting and teaching. Subsequently, they visited Liu Haisu's Chinese paintings in the college's Cuntian Pavilion. Dr. Rogers further inquired of Principal Liu about the origins and trends of Chinese art, as well as the highest principles and methods of Chinese painting. Mrs. Rogers also expressed her intention to engage in the study of Chinese painting. Mr. Liu explained the historical changes and evolution of Chinese art, and thoroughly elucidated the Six Principles of Chinese painting. Director Xu translated each point, and Dr. Rogers expressed great admiration. They lingered for two hours. Principal Liu then presented them with copies of his recent works and his lectures on the Six Principles at the University of Frankfurt in Germany. It was also arranged that Dr. Wu Jingxiong would accompany them to Mr. Liu's studio for further discussion on Friday evening.

Shanghai Education After January 28th (III) Shang 138

▲More Than 98,000 Students in the City Have Dropped Out of School

Three. Students Dropping Out of School 139

During the European War, even as the warring nations were shrouded in intense artillery fire, millions of young children diligently buried themselves in their studies. When faced with no other choice, they dug cellars to continue their education. During the Russo-Japanese War, Japan mobilized the entire nation, but elementary school teachers were absolutely not drawn into the vortex, remaining calmly in schools to train young citizens. They all recognized that students were the country's reserves, and reserves must be trained with utmost care. Looking back at our generally so-called reserves, what happened? Without a nationwide mobilization, but only a battle in one corner of Shanghai, the general reserves had almost nowhere to train and nothing to read. Until the end of April, when both sides ceased hostilities and loudly proclaimed peace, there were still nearly 100,000 students wandering astray. According to the reporter's analysis, their reasons for dropping out of school can be summarized in the following six points: 1. Watching the situation; 2. Economic difficulties; 3. Worry and fear; 4. Traffic obstructions; 5. Lack of good schools; 6. Family obstruction. These six points hindered their prospects and damaged the nation's vitality. Let's look at the number of students who dropped out of school. According to the statistics on schools, students, and teachers published by the Municipal Education Bureau in October of the 20th year, there were a total of 31 higher education institutions in the city, including 9 public schools and 24 private schools. The number of students in public schools was 2,671, and in private schools was 11,653, totaling 14,324. Among these, 516 university students dropped out from public schools, and 7,129 from private schools, totaling 7,645. The percentage of students who dropped out of school compared to the original number of students was 19% for public schools, 61% for private schools, and 52% for the entire student population. Why is the number of students dropping out of private schools nearly twice as high as that of public schools? The biggest reason may be that private schools charge higher fees. It is hoped that the government will pay attention to this and provide relief. According to the latest report from the Municipal Education Bureau, there are a total of 125 middle schools in the city, both public and private, with 28,514 students. The estimated number of students who dropped out this time is 15,000, accounting for more than 53% of the students enrolled. There are 774 elementary schools in the city, with more than 116,700 students. The total number of students who dropped out this time reached more than 75,500, accounting for more than 65% of the students enrolled. In total, more than 98,000 students dropped out of school. Seeing that nearly half of the students have dropped out of school is due to political instability, social immaturity, and families' lack of understanding, which allows so many promising young children to waste their time. The reporter knows that when Westerners travel to Shanghai, they still want to send their children to school for remedial studies in a very short period of time. In the current elementary schools, Western children often have short-term remedial classes for one or two weeks. Why is it not surprising in our country that students drop out of school for two months, three months, or even a year and a half? It is even more understandable when foreigners invade, and can be forgiven to an extraordinary degree. Commercial News

Gold Prices Before the Financial Swap 140

Plummeted by 19.5 Taels 141

▲US Maintained Silver Prices, UK Expressed Cooperation. Yesterday, the 12th, the price of gold plummeted sharply, with a small rebound. There was a difference of 12 taels throughout the day. In the end, the price dropped nearly 20 taels, which was due to the US proposal to maintain the sharply declining silver prices, the UK's expression of cooperation, and Hoover's endorsement of using silver coins to repay all war debts. Moreover, countries using the gold standard around the world are now abolishing it. Therefore, the silver market rose again yesterday. Various news spread in the market, and people were extremely fearful. The opening price fell sharply by 10 taels. Afterwards, the intake and outgoings of various parties varied, causing the market price to fluctuate slightly. However, the foreign exchange market was very loose and weakened again. The market situation was particularly depressed and almost collapsed. Suddenly, it broke through 710 taels, which was because the exchange rate was extremely tight and the banks' appetites were dull. It was unexpected that this low point would occur before the swap. The detailed record of the overall market is as follows:

▲The Opening Price Dropped 10 Taels The June opening price fell immediately by 10 taels and 2 qian, to 719 taels. Large bars were only long by 1/16 to 1/8. The silver price was 1/8, but private telegrams were large by 8/6, and the footing was poor. Citibank was making rapid progress. Next was 18.5 taels, followed by a 2-tael increase. Tongtaichang, Yifeng, and the Dalian Gang were all buying, while Tongfeng, Hengda, Tongcheng, Yuanheng, Hongkang, and Yongdeng were selling. It was likely that US dollars were sold at 31.625 yuan in early August, then half a yuan, and recently 1.25 yuan. From around 9:00, the price went from 20 taels to 17.5 taels, then to 20 taels and 0.05 qian. Subsequently, Hengxing, Yuanheng, Yushunli, Dadecheng, Fuchang, Zhifeng, and Yongqian Changxiang came to sell, and the US dollar weakened to 0.75 yuan in August. The English gold price was quoted at 18.375 to 18.4375, and the gold price plummeted by 6 taels. At 9:30, Yuanjing was at 14.5 taels, with a rebound of more than 1 tael, reaching 15 taels and 7 qian. The English gold price was quoted higher by 0.125, and the US dollar by 0.25. Then it retreated to 14.5 taels. Soon, Hengxing, Yifeng, Fuxing, Yongheng, Yushunli, and Dadecheng came to buy, and the exchange rate seemed stable, with the recent settlement at only 0.125. As a result, the price increased by 4.5 taels, reaching 19 taels at 10:20. Afterwards, Qianchangxiang, Hongkangyong, Richang, and others sold, suppressing the price by a small 3 taels and some change. However, there was a fluctuation of 2 taels in half an hour. The US dollar for August should have been sold at 0.625. Until 11:00, it was 15 taels and 8 qian. Suddenly, it increased by 2 taels, with a hedged purchase of 17 taels and 8 qian. However, the exchange rate was still loose, and the banks were unwilling to absorb more. The sellers in the market were still prevalent. It is estimated that Shunli, Bingxing, Zhaofeng, Changyuan, Tai, and others were selling heavily, so the price dropped by 4 taels, with a difference of only more than 1 tael. Until 11:50, it was 13 taels and 9 qian. Then the market closed at 14 taels, and the quoted price was changed to 793 taels, with a discount of 80 taels.

▲The Afternoon Market Collapsed The afternoon market opened at 13 taels and 5 qian, then at 15 taels and 5 qian. Because Fuyu Hengxing Yuanmao Yong and others bought, Yuanheng Fuchang Zhifeng Yongyuan Taikang Hengyu Qianchangxiang Futaiheng and others sold enthusiastically. Especially the US dollar became looser, and the banks initially absorbed August at 32.875 to 32.935, and then September at 2.0625 yuan, which was not easy to sell. Moreover, the Indian exchange rate was quoted large by four points, so the price plummeted by more than 5 taels, reaching 710 taels around 3:00. Afterwards, it seemed to rise by 2 taels, but there was a fluctuation of more than 1 tael. At 3:30, it was 12 taels and 4 qian. Because China Bank once absorbed August at 32 yuan, and September at 2.0625 yuan, the market fell into a slump again. Yifeng Yong Zhifeng Yong Qianchangxiang Fuchang and others were even more determined to sell, and the US dollar for September reached 2.1875 yuan. The market had an uncontrollable trend, and people were panicked and the atmosphere deteriorated. The price dropped another 4 taels, and finally ended at 08 taels and 3 qian at 4:00. At that time, short sellers and retail investors made up for the previous 1 tael, to 09 taels and 8 qian, with a slight increase of a few qian. At 4:30, it was 09 taels and 7 qian, a drastic drop of 19.5 taels compared to the previous day. According to the largest price of 20 taels and the smallest price of 08 taels and 3 qian in one day, there was a difference of 12 taels and 2 qian. The quoted price discounted 80 taels, and the final price was 83 or 84 taels. The book price was 14 taels, the interest supplement was 14 taels, and the red bar in the afternoon, plus 6 taels and 75 qian.

▲Sellers Prevailed The trading on the table was varied. According to statistics, Hengxing and Yifeng bought a total of 1,700 or 1,800 bars. Yuanmao Yong, Shunli, Wanxing, Tongtaichang, Taifengcheng, Wupin, and Yuankangxiang also bought. Zhifengyong, Yuantai, Fuchang, Yuanheng, Daxingyong, Futaiheng, Dakang, Hongkangyong, Yuhe, Qianchangxiang, and Mr. Wu, etc., were all selling short. Hengyu, Fuyu, Dadecheng, and others were very busy with transactions. In the afternoon, Hengxing, Fuyu, Shunli, Yuanmao Yong, and Wupin all bought. Wanxing, Zhifengyong, Fuchang, Yuanheng, Qianchangxiang, Yuantai, Futaiheng, and Hengyu all sold. Other firms had varied buy and sell orders.

New Silk Cocoons from Hangzhou Suburbs Enter the Market 151

▲Bad Weather Leads to Poor Cocoon Quality, Only 30% of Normal Harvest

In the Linping area of Hangzhou, farmers have greatly reduced the amount of silkworm eggs they are raising this spring, due to learning from the failure of last year's sericulture. In addition, the weather has been unfavorable, and the silkworms are in poor condition. Many were discarded due to the damage from the stuffy heat and extreme cold during the major molt. Although the new cocoons have entered the market, the cocoon production is poor, with only 30% of the normal harvest. The cocoons are of inferior quality, and only a few cocoon shops have opened for business. Improved varieties are priced at 25 to 30 yuan, and native cocoons are not being accepted. Many silkworm farmers are drying the cocoons themselves.

Stagnant Sales of Foreign Silk 152

Yesterday, the foreign silk market in Shanghai remained as stagnant as before. The European and American markets continue to be flooded with Japanese silk, imports are booming, and the factory price is still small. The price from New York is less than 500 taels, and the factory is still difficult to sell. Yesterday, only Yongxing imported 8 bales of spot goods of Mianzhou yellow raw silk, 24 to 3 threads, priced at 500 taels. Samsung imported 25 bales of Mianyang yellow silk, brand 3K, number 234, priced at 415 taels.

Sudden Drop of Over 10 Taels for High-Grade Tea 153

Yesterday, the situation in the foreign tea market, which has been attracting a lot of attention, was no longer the same as before. Although the Sui'an high-grade eyebrow green tea from the incoming firms had over a hundred new samples displayed, the foreign firms were not in a hurry because there were no ships departing recently, and most of them complained about the high price, and the negotiations ultimately failed. The local firms, such as Xiehe and Jinlong, slightly increased their purchases of high-grade eyebrow and needle eyebrow green teas, but the recognized price was much more stringent than before, and the market price plummeted by 14 to 15 taels. The tea merchants have all sent telegrams to stop the sharp rise in tea prices in the producing areas, so as to avoid repeating the mistakes of previous years.

Keemun Black Tea Arrives in Shanghai 154

Yesterday, Zhongxinchang, Rende, Yongshen, Yuanyuan and other tea firms had transported more than 200 boxes of Keemun black tea. The results of the brewing test show that the aroma and manufacturing method are better than last year, but because the amount is not much, it is necessary to wait for the large batch to arrive before the samples can be officially displayed.

New Developments of Tunxi Tea Firms 155

According to a survey conducted last month, the number of tea firms in Yanghu, Shuaikou, Liyang, Gaojian, Baishuxia and other places in Tunxi has reached more than 80. This month, merchants from Wuyi and Xiuning have moved to Tunxi because it is convenient for manufacturing and transportation. Recently, the total number of old and new tea firms in Tunxi has reached more than 100, and the market is unusually lively. As the new tea is about to be officially opened and priced, each firm is busy preparing cash to ship early. However, the recent ticket prices and cash, after the robbery of the Dakang and other tea firms, the market is tighter than before, and the firms are slightly affected.

Slight Drop in Keemun Tea Prices 156

Since the opening of Qi Fu autumn black tea the week before last, the price of Qi West tea has risen sharply from 95 yuan to 1120 yuan. The increase in the market is greater than before. The tea firms have been rushing to buy the first-class tea as the mountain households have reduced production this year, and they are now rushing to buy the second and third batches. However, due to the hot weather this week and the occasional hailstorms, it is not conducive to picking tea leaves. The sun-dried tea leaves are overly saturated with rain, making them hard and of poor quality, and the leaves are coarse. The tea firms are finding it difficult to supply the cash, so they are reducing their purchases and waiting for the weather to clear before buying more of the better-quality tea. The market price should be gradually decreasing with each batch, but due to the rush of tea firms to buy, the market has slightly increased. As a result, the cost of tea for the firms is higher than before.

▲End of May is Approaching

▲Money Industry Held Meeting Yesterday

The silver and money industries, with regard to the year-end accounts for the 20th year, are scheduled to have a general closing at the end of May. Now that the deadline is approaching, it is necessary to have some discussions. Also, regarding the issue of a two-day closure after the closing of accounts, it is heard that the banking industry advocates not stopping and continuing to operate as usual. The money industry is unable to rush to handle it due to procedural reasons and still intends to close for two days. However, because banks are unwilling to stop, money shops cannot be an exception. The Shanghai Municipal Government Lodges Protest Against Out-of-Bounds Road Construction in Western Shanghai 168

The Public Concession's Works Department has been constructing road surfaces beyond the boundary in the Anhe Temple Road and Qiaodun Road areas of Western Shanghai. The Public Security Bureau has reported the facts and details to the Municipal Government. The Secretariat of the Municipal Government yesterday made a special report and protested to the Works Department.

To the Public Concession Works Department:

Regarding the case of Mayor 交下 市 Public Security Bureau呈 一 件, stating that the second precinct of the sixth district reported that after the outbreak of the Sino-Japanese war on January 28, the Concession's Works Department took advantage of the government's lack of time to take care of the road rights, and secretly repaired the roads on various roads, and sent armed British soldiers to protect them and prevent passage. A total of five electric light poles were installed on Anhe Temple Road and other roads, and new coal slag was laid on the east and west ends of the road. New coal slag was laid on Qiaodun Road west to the east of the railway for two li. Fourteen electric light poles were installed. A new wooden bridge was built on the west end of Haige Road and Fukaison Road. The original wooden bridge in the middle of Qiaodun Road has been demolished, and the river has also been filled in. One-third of the Shuibang on Kaixuan Road has also been filled in. The above-mentioned roads have been secretly constructed and completed, and the situation of the secretly repaired roads should be reported for review. The reasons are the same. According to this, after investigation, the above-mentioned roads are outside the scope of the concession. Without the approval of this government, your bureau has arbitrarily paved the road surface of each road, filled in the river, built and unloaded bridges, and installed electric poles, which seriously impairs sovereignty. A protest is lodged accordingly, and it is hoped that you will investigate, transfer your attention, and reply.

Customs Suspends Issuance of Inner Port Special Licenses 169

▲Separate Reporting Method for Customs Clearance to Be Determined

Tang Haian, Superintendent of the Jianghai Customs, and Luo Fude, Tax Affairs Secretary, issued a joint announcement yesterday.

(Regarding the matter of joint announcements, the Customs has issued inner port special licenses and Jiangzhao licenses for Chinese merchant ships. Now, according to the government's clear order, the issuance will be suspended from June 1 of this year. From that date, all Chinese merchant ships should be cleared at the port of commerce. The agent or captain of the ship shall prepare a customs clearance application form, stating the ship's destination, route, and which regulations it is traveling under (Ordinary River Navigation Regulations, Inner Port River Navigation Regulations, or Special Jiang River Navigation Regulations) and submit it to the Customs for verification. Each Chinese merchant ship should also prepare a logbook to record the port where the ship clears customs, the destination, and all other itinerary matters. All detailed measures regarding this new chapter can be inquired about from the customs clearance officer of the General Affairs Section of this Customs. All ship merchants must abide by them. This is a special announcement.)

Banks Agree to Discount and Lend Against Maturing Public Debt Principal and Interest Coupons 170

▲Result of Negotiations by Coupon Holders

After the outbreak of the Shanghai War, all banks felt it difficult to discount bond principal and interest coupons due to financial relations and refused to do so. For this reason, the 内国 Public Debt Treasury Coupon Holders Association separately sent letters to the National Debt Fund Management Committee and the Bankers Association, requesting them to persuade the banks to make appropriate changes to facilitate turnover. Yesterday, the association and others have agreed with the Central, China, and Jiaotong Banks to make appropriate arrangements, and separately replied to the coupon holders association. The original letters are recorded as follows:

▲Reply from the National Debt Fund

Dear Sirs,

The transfer volume of the Jianghai Customs 25 attached tax National Treasury Coupon Fund Custody Committee is approved. The association has stated that the discounting of public debt treasury coupon principal and interest coupons is a necessary measure for coupon holders to turn around in finance. On the other hand, it is the most reliable loan for bankers, and the fact that the bond principal and interest fund is kept by your association proves that this loan can be recovered on time. However, it is difficult for coupon holders to discount bond principal and interest coupons to the bank, even for those for the current month. Coupon holders have no way to turn around, and bankers lose a reliable loan business, and the social economy is even more difficult to 활활. It seems that there should be a need for remedy. It is known that your association has close relationships with bankers. If you can discuss with the relevant banks to allow coupon holders to discount the bond principal and interest coupons that will mature before the stipulated 90 days according to the usual banking practice, it would be a great public sentiment. In addition to函 to the Shanghai Banking Association,函 should also be達 to inquire about the verification of the matter, and give a reply. The Central China and Jiaotong Banks have been函 and the three banks have replied that they are willing to handle the matter in accordance with the regulations. They will函 to inquire about the verification of the matter, and give a reply.

Sincerely,

Li Ming, Chairman of the 内国 Public Debt Treasury Coupon Holders Association.

Dear Sirs,

The letter of March 19 stated that since the Shanghai War has occurred, each bank has felt it difficult to承 handle the discounting of bond principal and interest coupons. The Association has been requested to discuss with the banks to accept the request of the holder of the domestic bond to discount the public debt treasury coupon principal and interest coupon 90 days before its maturity. After sending the 函 to the Central China and Jiaotong Banks, it has been approved and the 函 has been returned one after another. They are willing to酌量 酌量 the matter.

The 函 has been forwarded.

The Chinese Taxpayers Association of the Public Concession yesterday notified all taxpayers and sent letters to the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, the Citizens Federation, and other groups regarding the municipal general donation.

For the matter of the notice, the Japanese army invaded Shanghai. Residents in the Public Concession, especially in the Hongkou area north of the Suzhou River, suffered unknown losses. The Board of Directors attaches great importance to the matters mentioned in your Association's letter of April 12. Labor Union and Workers' Association Host All Sectors 172

▲ Report on the Proposal to Consolidate the Postal Foundation ▲ All Sectors Willing to Assist Shanghai Postal Workers' Union with Real Strength The Labor Union and Workers' Association yesterday held a reception for all sectors at the Yipinxian Auditorium to report on the fundamental significance of the proposal to consolidate the postal foundation and its recent progress. Over two hundred people attended, including Wang Xiaolai, Lin Kanghou, Chu Huiseng, and Pan Gongzhan. Lu Jingshi and Fu Dewei, two comrades from the two associations, gave reports. Lai Zi Chu Huiseng, Pan Gongzhan, Lin Kanghou, Ren Jinping, Shen Junru, Hu Fengxiang, and Li Yongxiang delivered speeches, expressing their deep sympathy for the postal workers' current movement and their willingness to support the two associations with the strength of the people, urging the government to realize the proposal. The atmosphere was very enthusiastic. The reports and speeches are listed below: ▲ Group representatives attended the City Chamber of Commerce (Wang Xiaolai), the Bankers' Association (Lin Kanghou), the Money Trade Association (Qin Runqing), the Lawyers' Association (Shen Junru, Li Zuyu, Yu Congdao), the Accountants' Association (Yu Xiji), the Citizens' Federation (Hu Fengxiang, Zhang Yichen), the Taxpaying Chinese Association (Chu Huiseng), the National Salvation Federation of Various Groups (Yin Zhiling), the United Business Circles Association (Wu Zhihao), the General Labor Union (Zhou Xuexiang, Yu Xianting, Li Yongxiang), the Shen Bao (Shi Liangcai, Ling Qihan), the Chen Bao (Pan Gongzhan), the Dalu Bao (Zhang Zhuping, Ren Jinping), and representatives from over two hundred organizations including the Xinwen Bao, the Shibao, the Shishi Xinbao, the Telecommunications Workers' Union, the Fourth District Cigarette Workers' Union, the Ninth District Soap and Pharmaceutical Industry Union, various news agencies, and various labor unions. All members of the two associations were responsible for hosting. ▲ Chairman's Report Chairman Lu Jingshi reported, saying that he was very pleased to have leaders from all sectors attend today. The purpose of inviting everyone here today is to take this opportunity to report to you the significance of our association's consolidation of the postal foundation and to ask for your sympathy and support. The purpose of this movement is threefold: first, to merge the Savings and Remittance Bureau; second, to stop subsidizing airline expenses; and third, to maintain the administrative and economic independence of the post office. The separate establishment of the Savings and Remittance Bureau endangers the postal system itself and the public's savings. Since its establishment, we have been requesting its merger. As for airlines, our association believes that the government should allocate funds to operate them. The postal service is in dire economic straits and cannot afford to subsidize them. The implementation of postal administrative and accounting independence is the main reason for postal prosperity. Once it is not maintained, the postal service will inevitably be disturbed by corrupt officials. These three points are the fundamental purpose of this movement. We deeply believe in the natural duty of serving society. Seeing the deterioration of the postal environment, we have to be pioneers for the people, loudly call for action, and rise up to fight. We firmly believe that the revolutionary authorities will deeply understand public opinion and be happy to implement it. At the same time, we are confident that our purpose is bright and that even if there are other forces deliberately obstructing and attempting to destroy the postal service with thirty years of honor, our association and more than 30,000 employees will not hesitate to make any sacrifices to deal with them. After finishing his speech, he raised his glass to pay respects. Comrade Fu Dewei added that in the past ten years, the postal service has been allocated nearly 20 million in public funds by the Ministry of Communications. If the postal service had implemented special accounting, it would still be able to cover the deficit of more than 4 million this year. Why increase postal rates? Therefore, learning from past mistakes, we believe that consolidating the postal service's economic and administrative foundation is a fundamental way to save the postal service. Otherwise, not only will this postal rate increase not be canceled, but it will be difficult to guarantee that it will not increase again in two or three years. The future of the postal service is very dangerous, and the burden on the people will increase without limit. Our current movement is purely for the people and for the entire transportation industry, without any other purpose. We are confident that we will receive deep assistance from all sectors. ▲ Guest Speeches Chu Huiseng first delivered a speech on behalf of the representatives, saying that although the public actively opposed the postal rate increase, the government still ignored everything and resolutely increased it, which violated public opinion. The plan proposed by the postal workers is a fundamental plan to save the postal service. In the position of the people, we must urge its realization to achieve the purpose of consolidating the postal service and reducing the burden on the people. Pan Gongzhan said that the postal service and the customs were both founded by foreigners, resulting in today's achievements. However, after the postal rights were taken back, the government hastily bureaucratized the postal service and established a Savings and Remittance Bureau, disrupting postal administration. It is truly painful to say. In order to maintain the postal service and protect the interests of the people, we should first advocate that the Savings and Remittance Bureau be merged into the General Post Office. This matter not only requires the support of postal workers, but also the people should rise up and fight together for their own vital interests. Later, Ren Jinping, Li Yongxiang, Lin Kanghou, Hu Fengxiang, Shen Junru, and others delivered speeches one after another, and the situation was very enthusiastic. During the meeting, the representatives gave concrete directions for future movements and provided assistance with real strength. ▲ Chairman's Reply At the end, Lu Jingshi replied, saying that he was extremely grateful for the guidance and enthusiastic support of all the gentlemen. Our association and 30,000 postal workers across the country will resolutely fight to protect the postal service and strive for the benefit of all the people, even if it means going through fire and water, we will not hesitate to die. The meeting ended at 10 p.m. Minhang Chamber of Commerce

Telegram Requesting Exemption from Increased Business Tax Rate 173

The Minhang Chamber of Commerce telegraphed to the Nanjing Yuan and Ministry, stating: "To the Nanjing Executive Yuan, Legislative Yuan, and Ministry of Industry: It is reported that the Jiangsu Province amended the Business Tax Regulations, uniformly levying 10 per mille based on business volume or capital amount, which is inconsistent with the Business Tax Law promulgated by the Central Government. National laws and regulations are the standards for handling affairs. If there is a slight compromise, it would violate the original intention of legislation. Moreover, the business tax is only to compensate for the local revenue after the abolition of likin. It was originally a measure taken by the government out of necessity and is understood by our merchants. However, the originally set tax rate exceeded the provisions of the likin abolition meeting. Since the tax was levied one year ago, the revenue has been meager. Although it is affected by natural disasters, man-made disasters, internal and external troubles, the excessive tax rate and the merchants' inability to adapt are also the main reasons for this. The Jiangsu Provincial Department of Finance, due to the shortage of tax revenue, will steeply increase the tax rate several times. At this time, when the people are poor and businesses are declining and the market is sluggish, the existing regulations are already heavy and unbearable for merchants. To say that this can increase revenue is to put the cart before the horse. The late Premier attached importance to people's livelihood, and the government inherited his legacy and announced it to the world. Regarding the heavy taxes set by Jiangsu Province, we earnestly request the implementation of the virtue of likin abolition and saving the people (submit to the Executive Yuan) to stop the increase, so as to respect the legal system and relieve merchants' difficulties. Zhang Jingling, Acting Chairman of the Shanghai County Minhang Chamber of Commerce, kowtows. True Seal. Color Printing Association.

Requesting Exemption from Business Tax Again 174

The Color Printing Association sent a letter to the City Chamber of Commerce, stating: "Regarding the business tax in the autumn and winter seasons of last year, because our industry was affected by the war, either suffering from tragic disasters or business stagnation, at this time of commercial hardship, it is really unbearable to bear this burden. Our association had submitted the situation in a letter on March 22, requesting that it be forwarded to the municipal government for concurrent exemption. Although various industries have now reopened, the factories and stores of our industry in the war zone have been completely destroyed and are awaiting relief. Those who have not been affected have also suffered from economic depression due to prolonged work stoppages, and there are often requests for assistance from the association. Seeing this situation, our association really cannot bear to urge the payment of this tax again. After repeated consideration, the only thing we can do is to still earnestly request your association to truthfully forward the situation to the municipal government, showing consideration for commercial hardship, and approve the exemption of the business tax for the autumn and winter seasons of last year, so as to relieve the difficulties of the merchants. We express our sincere gratitude."
